			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of dialling codes in Germany</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">

<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png/220px-Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png" width="220" height="284" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png/330px-Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png/440px-Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="646" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Telefonvorwahlbereiche-Deutschland.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Area code zones in Germany</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/Country_calling_code" class="mw-redirect" title="Country calling code">Country Code</a>: +49</b><br />
<b><a href="/wiki/International_Call_Prefix" class="mw-redirect" title="International Call Prefix">International Call Prefix</a>: 00</b><br />
<b><a href="/wiki/Trunk_Prefix" class="mw-redirect" title="Trunk Prefix">Trunk Prefix</a>: 0</b></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Area_code" class="mw-redirect" title="Area code">Area codes</a> in <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> (<a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a> <i>Vorwahl</i>) have two to five digits, not counting the leading trunk access code 0. The leading 0 must be dialed when calling from within Germany and must be omitted when calling from abroad. When calling via fixed networks within the same area, the area code is not required. In general, shorter area codes are assigned to larger cities, and longer area codes to smaller towns. Private telephone numbers are usually inversely long: those in larger cities have seven or eight digits, while those in smaller towns may have as few as three or four digits. The first digit (after the <a href="/wiki/Leading_zero" title="Leading zero">leading zero</a>) is determined by region: area codes beginning (0)2 are found in the west, those with (0)3 in the east, those with (0)4 in the north, those with (0)5 in the north central part, those with (0)6 in the south central part, those with (0)7 in the southwest, those with (0)8 in the south and the 9s are found in the southeast.</p>
<p>(0)1 are special numbers such as mobile phones (015, 016, 017), shared cost service (0180), televoting numbers (013) and 010 for dial-around services. The former codes 0130 for free phone numbers and 0190 for premium-rate numbers are now moved to 0800 and 0900 to meet international standards. 0700 is used for personal national phone numbers.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="01">01</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: 01">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Prefix 01 is used for special numbers, and is not tied to a geographic area.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="010">010</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 010">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="015">015</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 015">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li>015 mobile phones

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="03">03</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 03">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>All of former <a href="/wiki/East_Germany" title="East Germany">East Germany</a> and Berlin</p>
<p>East Germany was using +37 before <a href="/wiki/German_reunification" title="German reunification">the reunification</a>. After reunification, East Germany was merged into the existing (West) German numbering plan. Since all areas except 03 were already used, all of former East Germany needed to be merged into 03, causing numbers and area codes in the 03 area to be longer than those in the rest of Germany: Many area codes in the 03 area are 5-digit while the maximum in the rest of Germany is 4 digits</p>
<h3><span id="030&#160;–_Berlin"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="030.C2.A0.E2.80.93_Berlin">030&#160;– Berlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 030 – Berlin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="09">09</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=215" title="Edit section: 09">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Remark">Remark</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=216" title="Edit section: Remark">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>These area codes were changed in February 1997 in order to allow service 0900 numbers:</p>
<ul>
<li>09002 → 09090 Rain (Lech)</li>
<li>09003 → 09080 Harburg (Schwaben)</li>
<li>09004 → 09070 Tapfheim</li>
<li>09005 → 09084 Bissingen (Schwaben)</li>
<li>09006 → 09078 Mertingen</li>
<li>09007 → 09097 Marxheim</li>
<li>09008 → 09089 Bissingen-Unterringingen</li>
<li>09009 → 09099 Kaisheim</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="090">090</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_dialling_codes_in_Germany&amp;action=edit&amp;section=217" title="Edit section: 090">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li>0900-1 premium-rate information services</li>

<li>0900-9 premium-rate <a href="/wiki/Dialer" title="Dialer">dialer</a></li>
</ul>
